                                        FluffyTermExpectationOutcome::EqsSort(
                                            TermUniverse(
                                                1,
                                            ),
                                        ),
                                    ),
                                ),
                            },
                        },
                    ],
                },
                first_unresolved_expectation: 0,
            },
        },
        return_ty: None,
        self_ty: Some(
            EtherealTerm(`f64`),
        ),
    },
]
